    <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        const boxes = document.querySelectorAll('.saboxplugin-wrap');
        if (boxes.length > 1) {
            // Hide all except the last one
            boxes.forEach((box, index) => {
                if (index < boxes.length - 1) {
                    box.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        }
        // If there's only one box, do nothing
    });

	// 	Dark/Light Mode Toggle
	const toggle = document.querySelectorAll('.theme-switch');

	// Default theme: dark
	if (localStorage.getItem('theme') === 'light') {
		htmlEl.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
	} else {
		htmlEl.removeAttribute('data-theme'); // stays in dark
	}
	toggle.forEach((item) => {

		item.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
			e.preventDefault();
			if (htmlEl.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'light') {
				htmlEl.removeAttribute('data-theme');
				localStorage.setItem('theme', 'dark');
			} else {
				htmlEl.setAttribute('data-theme', 'light');
				localStorage.setItem('theme', 'light');
			}
		});
	})

	// 	Header Searchbar
	jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
		// Show search bar on icon click
		$('#search_icon').click(function(e) {
			e.stopPropagation(); // Prevent bubbling to document
			$('#headr_search').addClass('show-searchbar');
			$(this).css({
				'transition': 'opacity 0.3s ease-in-out',
				'pointer-events': 'none',
				'opacity': '0'
			});
		});

		// Hide search bar when clicking outside
		$(document).on('click', function(e) {
			if (!$(e.target).closest('#headr_search, #search_icon').length) {
				$('#headr_search').removeClass('show-searchbar');
				$('#search_icon').css({
					'pointer-events': '',
					'opacity': '1'
				});
			}
		});

		// 	Menu icon hide/show 
		menu_open = $('#mobile_menu_open .elementor-icon');
		menu_close = $('#mobile_menu_close .elementor-icon');

		function MenuPopupShow() {
			$('#mobile_menu_open').hide();
			$('#mobile_menu_close').show();
			$('body').css({"overflow": "hidden"})
			$('#popup-menu').addClass('menu-popup-active');
		}
		
		function MenuPopupHide() {
			$('#mobile_menu_close').hide();
			$('#mobile_menu_open').show();
			$('body').css({"overflow": ""})
			$('#popup-menu').removeClass('menu-popup-active');
		}
		menu_open.click(function(){
			MenuPopupShow();
		})
// 		$('#mobile-searchPopup_menu .elementor-icon').click(function(){
// 			MenuPopupShow();
// 		})

		menu_close.click(function(){
			MenuPopupHide();
		})
		$('#mobile-search-popup-button').click(function(){
			MenuPopupHide();
		})
		
		// close when clicking outside
// $(document).on('click', function(e) {
// 	if (window.matchMedia("(max-width: 767px)").matches) {
// 		if (!$(e.target).closest('#mobile_menu_open, #mobile_menu_close, .mobile_menu_popup').length) {
// 			$('#mobile_menu_close').hide();
// 			$('#mobile_menu_open').show();
// 		}
// 	}
// });

		/* Off-canvas search bar */
		$('#offCan_search_icon .elementor-icon').click(function() {
			$('#offCan_searchBar').toggleClass('show-searchbar');
		})

	})
	
</script>
